A JSTree version of my Perl.Wiki

CPAN::MetaCurator V 1.27. 2026-07-22T14:53:02

My home page, for downloading Perl.Wiki.html

Notes:
⊕ Nodes just under the root ('MetaCurator') are called Topics. Paragraphs is the TiddlyWiki equivalent.
⊕ Tokens like [[XS]] indicate a topic (a TiddlyWiki paragraph name), not a Perl module.
⊕ Almost all leaf node are links. Use a middle-button click to open the link in another tab.
⊕ The code does not yet cleanly handle special cases such as the FAQ or pre-formatted paras.
⊕ Also, cases where the para is just a 'See also' are not yet clean.

⊕ My other module, CPAN::MetaPackages, builds & ships an SQLite db containing 02packages.details.txt.
⊕ Most recent version of 02packages.details.txt used: Last-Updated: Sun, 14 Jun 2026 23:17:02 GMT .
⊕ Acronyms: 271. CPAN modules: 265554. Wiki modules: 5973. Topics: 214. Unclassified: 5354.
